MISSION - Paris Blues (1961)</a></div><div class="_6m7 _3bt9">Vince selects a romantic drama set in 1961 Paris, France starring Sidney Poitier and Diahann Carroll alongside Paul Newman and Joanne Woodward and defends it as a quintessential Black film. GUEST:

Rich Conte  &#064;richconte .

Proud Dad, Information Architect, Rockabilly fan and lucky husband of a nice Southern girl. Also Producer and Host of &#064;TechLifePod podcast.

 Charleston SC

SHOW  DESCRIPTION:

Earlier this afternoon the NBA Trade Deadline officially expired. So now Celtics Fan&#039;s will know what their team will be for the rest of the 2016/2017 season and in the Playoffs as the Celtics try to make it past round 1 this season. The Celtics were linked to several rumors over the last few weeks involving several big name players. From trades that would have the Celtics getting superstar players to trades that would see the Celtics get involved as a 3rd team to help a trade go through and allow them to pick up some of the pieces they needed to add. The Celtics coming into this trade deadline needed help in the rebounding department so they needed a big man and that was something the teams players and coaches admitted. Did Danny Ainge manage to get that done? Did the Celtics add a big name player to help them draw closer to the Cavaliers and Raptors in terms of star power and make themselves more of a major threat to knock off the Raptors and Cavs this season and prove they could be the team in the East to prevent a Cavaliers/Warriors NBA Finals 3 from happening. We will discuss what happened earlier today with our guest Rich Conte of the TechLifePod Podcast will join us.
